                                    Star Jasmine Overgrown? When and How to Prune for Best Results                                    <span><p>Quick Answer: Pruning Overgrown Star Jasmine Prune star jasmine (Trachelospermum jasminoides) immediately after flowering finishes in late summer (August-September). Cut back overgrown stems by up to two-thirds, removing old woody growth to encourage fresh flowering shoots. 				<div class="wrap">
